# Minorities Menu
country_event = {
	id = glp_save_edit_events.3
	title = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTNAME3"
	desc = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTDESC3"
	picture = HRE_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
	}

	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTMINORITIESZZ1"
	}
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTMINORITIESA01"
		FROM = {
			save_event_target_as = MJ_minorities
		}
		country_event = { id = glp_save_edit_events_MINORITIESADD.1 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTMINORITIESA02"
		FROM = {
			remove_event_target = MJ_minorities
		}
		country_event = { id = glp_save_edit_events_MINORITIESREMOVE.1 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTMINORITIESA03"
		FROM = {
			save_event_target_as = MJ_minorities
		}
		country_event = { id = glp_save_edit_events_MINORITIESAPROOVE.1 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTMINORITIESA04"
		FROM = {
			save_event_target_as = MJ_minorities
		}
		country_event = { id = glp_save_edit_events_MINORITIESDISAPROOVE.1 }
	}
}

# Change Province Religion Event

country_event = {
	id = glp_save_edit_events.24
	title = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTNAME24"
	desc = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTDESC24"
	picture = HRE_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
	}

	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTOPTZZ1"
	}

	#GLP 2024 INQUISITION
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTOPTAA24"
		trigger = {
			is_religion_enabled = corinite
			FROM = { 
				NOT = { religion = corinite }
			}
		}
		FROM = { change_religion = corinite }
	}

	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTOPTA24"
		trigger = {
			FROM = { 
				NOT = { religion = regent_court }
			}
		}
		FROM = { change_religion = regent_court }
	}

	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTOPTB24"
		trigger = {
			FROM = { 
				NOT = { religion = dalcabba }
			}
		}
		FROM = { change_religion = dalcabba }
	}

	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTOPTC24"
		trigger = {
			FROM = { 
				NOT = { religion = infernal_court }
			}
		}
		FROM = { change_religion = infernal_court }
	}

# Release Province

country_event = {
	id = glp_save_edit_events.26
	title = none
	desc = none
	picture = none
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = glp_release_province_owner
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_core_country = { exists = no }
					}
					random_core_country = {
						limit = {
							exists = no
						}
						FROM = { 
							cede_province = PREV 
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					random_core_country = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { has_country_flag = glp_release_province_owner }
						}
						FROM = { 
							cede_province = PREV 
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = glp_release_province_owner
				}
				clr_country_flag = glp_release_province_owner 
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
	}
}

# Release all possible countries

country_event = {
	id = glp_save_edit_events.27
	title = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTNAME27"
	desc = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTDESC27"
	picture = HRE_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
	}

	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTOPTA27"
	}

	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTOPTB27"
		FROM = {
			owner = {
				release_all_possible_countries = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = glp_save_edit_events.29
	title = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTNAME29"
	desc = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTDESC29"
	picture = HRE_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
	}

	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTOPTA29"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = "glp_quest_reward_colonist"
			}
			tooltip = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "glp_quest_reward_colonist"
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
		}
		if ={
			limit ={
				has_country_modifier = "glp_quest_reward_settler"
			}
			tooltip = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "glp_quest_reward_settler"
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
		}
		if ={
			limit ={
				has_country_modifier = "glp_quest_reward_missionary"
			}
			tooltip = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "glp_quest_reward_missionary"
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
		}
		if ={
			limit ={
				has_country_modifier = "glp_quest_reward_conversion"
			}
			tooltip = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "glp_quest_reward_conversion"
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
		}
		if ={
			limit ={
				OR = {
					has_country_modifier = "glp_quest_reward_mercenary"
					has_country_modifier = "glp_quest_reward_mercenary_inf"
					has_country_modifier = "glp_quest_reward_mercenary_art"
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = glp_new_merc_company
			tooltip = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "glp_quest_reward_mercenary"
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
		}
		if ={
			limit ={
				has_country_modifier = "glp_quest_reward_trader"
			}
			tooltip = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "glp_quest_reward_trader"
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
		}
		if ={
			limit ={
				has_country_modifier = "glp_quest_reward_stability"
			}
			tooltip = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "glp_quest_reward_stability"
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
		}
		if ={
			limit ={
				has_country_modifier = "glp_quest_reward_diplomatic"
			}
			tooltip = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "glp_quest_reward_diplomatic"
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Merc Disband Events

country_event = {
	id = glp_save_edit_events.30
	title = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTNAME30"
	desc = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTDESC30"
	picture = HRE_eventPicture

	#is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		#has_country_flag = glp_merc_quest_reward_flag
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = "glp_quest_reward_mercenary" }
		any_hired_mercenary_company = {
			template = glp_kingts_of_round
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 90
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_hired_mercenary_company = {
				limit = {
					template = glp_kingts_of_round
				}
				save_event_target_as = glp_kingts_of_round_disband_target
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTOPTA30"
		#clr_country_flag = glp_merc_quest_reward_flag
		custom_tooltip = glp_merc_company_expired
		if = {
			limit = { has_saved_event_target = glp_kingts_of_round_disband_target }
			event_target:glp_kingts_of_round_disband_target = {
				disband_mercenary_company = THIS
			}
		}
	}
}

# Spawn Broceliande

country_event = {
	id = glp_save_edit_events.33
	title = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTNAME33"
	desc = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTDESC33"
	picture = HRE_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
	}
	
	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTOPTA33"
	}

	option = { 
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTOPTB33"
		random_province = {
			limit = {
				region = cascadia_region
				is_empty = yes
				has_port = yes
			}
			add_core = BRO
			cede_province = ROOT
			change_culture = welsh
			change_religion = catholic
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					ai = no
					#culture_group = germanic
				}
				add_permanent_claim = PREV
				discover_province = PREV
			}
		}
		ROOT = { release = BRO }
		BRO = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "glp_broceliande_modifier"
				duration = -1
			}
			adopt_reform_progress = ROOT
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Morgan"
				dynasty = "Le Fay"
				age = 1112
				adm = 6
				dip = 3
				mil = 6
				claim = 100
				female = yes
			}
			add_ruler_personality = immortal_personality
			if = {
				limit = {
					mil_tech = 7
				}
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.7
						cavalry = 0.1
						artillery = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.7
						cavalry = 0.3
					}
				}
			}
			capital_scope = {
				add_permanent_province_modifier = {
					name = "glp_broceliande_capital_modifier"
					duration = -1
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_building = fort_15th
					}
					remove_building = fort_15th
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_building = fort_16th
					}
					remove_building = fort_16th
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_building = fort_17th
					}
					remove_building = fort_17th
				}
				add_building = fort_18th
				add_base_tax = 15
				add_base_production = 15
				add_base_manpower = 15
			}
			change_government = monarchy
			add_government_reform = feudalism_reform
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTOPTC33"
		FROM ={
			add_core = BRO
			cede_province = ROOT
			change_culture = welsh
			change_religion = catholic
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					ai = no
					#culture_group = germanic
				}
				add_permanent_claim = PREV
				discover_province = PREV
			}
		}
		ROOT = { release = BRO }
		BRO = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "glp_broceliande_modifier"
				duration = -1
			}
			adopt_reform_progress = ROOT
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Morgan"
				dynasty = "Le Fay"
				age = 1112
				adm = 6
				dip = 3
				mil = 6
				claim = 100
				female = yes
			}
			add_ruler_personality = immortal_personality
			if = {
				limit = {
					mil_tech = 7
				}
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.7
						cavalry = 0.1
						artillery = 0.2
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				capital_scope = {
					build_to_forcelimit = {
						infantry = 0.7
						cavalry = 0.3
					}
				}
			}
			capital_scope = {
				add_permanent_province_modifier = {
					name = "glp_broceliande_capital_modifier"
					duration = -1
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_building = fort_15th
					}
					remove_building = fort_15th
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_building = fort_16th
					}
					remove_building = fort_16th
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_building = fort_17th
					}
					remove_building = fort_17th
				}
				add_building = fort_18th
				add_base_tax = 15
				add_base_production = 15
				add_base_manpower = 15
			}
			change_government = monarchy
			add_government_reform = feudalism_reform
		}
	}
}

# Comet Sighted Event Change

country_event = {
	id = glp_save_edit_events.34
	title = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTNAME34"
	desc = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTDESC34"
	picture = HRE_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
	}

	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTOPTA34"
	}

	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTOPTB34"
		custom_tooltip = glp_comets_provide_stab_tt
		set_global_flag = glp_comets_provide_stab_flag
	}

	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTOPTC34"
		custom_tooltip = glp_comets_remove_stab_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = glp_comets_provide_stab_flag
			}
			clr_global_flag = glp_comets_provide_stab_flag
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = glp_save_edit_events.35
	title = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTNAME35"

		}
		set_country_flag = glp_npc_advisor_overlord

#PROVINCE BUILDUP
country_event = {
	id = glp_save_edit_events.71
	title = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTNAME71"
	desc = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTDESC71"
	picture = DIET_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
	}

	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTBATZZ1"
	}
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			save_event_target_as = glp_builder_nation
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = glp_save_edit_events.EVTBATA01
		
		country_event = { id = glp_save_edit_events.72 }
	}
	option = {
		name = glp_save_edit_events.EVTBATA02
		country_event = { id = glp_save_edit_events.73 }
	}
	option = {
		name = glp_save_edit_events.EVTBATA03
		country_event = { id = glp_save_edit_events.74 }
	}
	option = {
		name = glp_save_edit_events.EVTBATA04
		country_event = { id = glp_save_edit_events.75 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTBATA05"
		FROM = {
			remove_all_buildings = yes
		}
		clear_global_event_target = glp_builder_nation
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = glp_save_edit_events.72
	title = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTNAME72"
	desc = "glp_save_edit_events.EVTDESC72"
	picture = CITY_DEVELOPMENT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
	}
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.BUILDINGZZ1"
	}
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.BUILDINGA01"
		event_target:glp_builder_nation = {
			add_building = temple
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.BUILDINGA02"
		event_target:glp_builder_nation = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_building = temple
				}
				remove_building = temple
				add_building = cathedral
			}
			else = {
				add_building = cathedral
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.BUILDINGA03"
		event_target:glp_builder_nation = {
			add_building = workshop
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.BUILDINGA04"
		event_target:glp_builder_nation = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_building = workshop
				}
				remove_building = workshop
				add_building = counting_house
			}
			else = {
				add_building = counting_house
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.BUILDINGA05"
		event_target:glp_builder_nation = {
			add_building = marketplace
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.BUILDINGA06"
		event_target:glp_builder_nation = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_building = marketplace
				}
				remove_building = marketplace
				add_building = trade_depot
			}
			else = {
				add_building = trade_depot
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.BUILDINGA07"
		event_target:glp_builder_nation = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_building = trade_depot
				}
				remove_building = trade_depot
				add_building = stock_exchange
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_building = marketplace
				}
				remove_building = marketplace
				add_building = stock_exchange
			}
			else = {
				add_building = stock_exchange
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.BUILDINGA08"
		event_target:glp_builder_nation = {
			add_building = courthouse
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.BUILDINGA09"
		event_target:glp_builder_nation = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_building = courthouse
				}
				remove_building = courthouse
				add_building = town_hall
			}
			else = {
				add_building = town_hall
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.BUILDINGA10"
		event_target:glp_builder_nation = {
			add_building = university
		}
	}
	#Dirt Roads
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.BUILDINGA11"
		event_target:glp_builder_nation = {
			add_building = early_road
		}
	}
	#Gravel Roads
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.BUILDINGA12"
		event_target:glp_builder_nation = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_building = early_road
				}
				remove_building = early_road
				add_building = gravel_road
			}
			else = {
				add_building = gravel_road
			}
		}
	}
	#Cobbelstone Roads
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.BUILDINGA13"
		event_target:glp_builder_nation = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_building = gravel_road
				}
				remove_building = gravel_road
				add_building = royal_road
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_building = early_road
				}
				remove_building = early_road
				add_building = royal_road
			}
			else = {
				add_building = royal_road
			}
		}
	}
	#Dwarven Roads
	option = {
		name = "glp_save_edit_events.BUILDINGA14"
		event_target:glp_builder_nation = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_building = gravel_road
				}
				remove_building = gravel_road
				add_building = macadam_road
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_building = early_road
				}
				remove_building = early_road

#The last reflection
country_event = {
	id = glp_save_edit_events_NUKE.1
	title = glp_save_edit_events_NUKE.EVTNAME1
	desc = glp_save_edit_events_NUKE.EVTDESC1
	picture = BIG_STAR_IN_SKY_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
	}

	option = {
		name = glp_save_edit_events_NUKE.EVTOPTZZ1
		hidden_effect = {
			clear_global_event_target = MJ_nuke
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = glp_save_edit_events_NUKE.EVTOPTA01
		event_target:MJ_nuke = { owner = { country_event = { id = glp_save_edit_events_NUKE.2 } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = glp_save_edit_events_NUKE.EVTOPTA02
		event_target:MJ_nuke = { owner = { country_event = { id = glp_save_edit_events_NUKE.3 } } }
	}
}

#It exploded...
country_event = {
	id = glp_save_edit_events_NUKE.3
	title = glp_save_edit_events_NUKEEXPLODED.EVTNAME1
	desc = glp_save_edit_events_NUKEEXPLODED.EVTDESC1
	picture = BIG_STAR_IN_SKY_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:MJ_nuke = {
				add_devastation = 100
				if = {
					limit = { base_tax = 2 }
					set_base_tax = 1
				}
				if = {
					limit = { base_production = 2 }
					set_base_production = 1
				}
				if = {
					limit = { base_manpower = 2 }
					set_base_manpower = 1
				}
				kill_units = {
					who = enemy
				}
				kill_units = {
					who = owner
				} 
				kill_units = {
					who = controller
				}
				remove_all_buildings = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = glp_save_edit_events_NUKEEXPLODED.EVTOPTA01
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clear_global_event_target = MJ_nuke
		}
	}
}
